Req-489: if the steering wheel angle whose index exceeds 9 is above the sailing termination within at most 9 seconds for at least 19 seconds ,  the steering wheel angle shall be set to [True]  every at most 9 seconds within at most 26 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the steering wheel angle, is above, [the sailing termination, ], if the steering wheel angle is above the sailing termination ),
subComp(hidden, the steering wheel angle, whose, index, exceeds, [9, ], the steering wheel angle whose index exceeds 9 ),
subComp(pre-time, within, at most, 9, seconds, [], within at most 9 seconds),
subComp(v-time, for, at least, 19, seconds, [], for at least 19 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the steering wheel angle, shall be set, [[True], ], the steering wheel angle shall be set to [True]),
subComp(in-time, every, at most, 9, seconds, [], every at most 9 seconds),
subComp(pre-time, within, at most, 26, seconds, [], within at most 26 seconds)
] )

]
